                China plans to send Uygur Muslims from Xinjiang re-education camps to work in other parts of country
            </h1><div class="info__subHeadline" data-v-3c0c8cda><div data-v-3c0c8cda><ul class="generic-article__summary--ul content--ul" data-v-c100079c data-v-3c0c8cda>
<li class="generic-article__summary--li content--li" data-v-c100079c>Inmates who have undergone compulsory re-education programme to be moved to other parts of China under job placement scheme delayed by Covid-19 outbreak</li>
<li class="generic-article__summary--li content--li" data-v-c100079c>Critics have said the camps are a move to eradicate cultural and religious identity but Beijing has defended them as way of boosting job opportunities and combating Islamic radicalisation</li>
</ul></div></div><a href="/topics/xinjiang" class="info__topic topic" data-v-3c0c8cda><div class="topic__title" data-v-3c0c8cda>Topic |
